                    background-position: left;"></div><button id="close-pc-btn-handler" class="ot-close-icon" aria-label="Close"></button></div><!-- Close Button --><div id="ot-pc-content" class="ot-pc-scrollbar"><h2 id="ot-pc-title">Do Not Sell My Personal Information</h2><div id="ot-pc-desc">The California Consumer Privacy Act (CCPA) permits California residents, or their authorized agents, to opt out of the sale of their personal information to third parties. Please visit <a href="https://privacy.thewaltdisneycompany.com/en/current-privacy-policy/your-california-privacy-rights/" target="_blank" class="Your" california="" privacy="" rights="">Your California Privacy Rights</a>  for more information about California residents rights and our privacy practices.</div><section class="ot-sdk-row ot-cat-grp"><h3 id="ot-category-title"></h3><div class="ot-cat-item ot-always-active-group" data-optanongroupid="C0001"><!-- Group name --><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-C0001">Technically Necessary</h4><div class="ot-always-active"></div><!-- Group description --><p class="ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-C0001">Technically necessary to provide this service or other features.</p></div><div class="ot-cat-item" data-optanongroupid="SPD_BG"><!-- Group name --><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-SPD_BG">Sale of Personal Data</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-SPD_BG" id="ot-group-id-SPD_BG" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="SPD_BG" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-SPD_BG"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-SPD_BG"><span class="ot-switch-nob"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Sale of Personal Data</span></label> </div><!-- Group description --><p class="ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-SPD_BG">When you visit this website, we and our partners may collect certain information about you, your devices, and your behaviour, and sell this information to third parties to provide you with certain advertising on this site and across the web tailored to you and your interests.  You can use the opt out toggle above to opt out of the sale of your personal information, as defined by the CCPA, of certain advertising on this site. If you opt out on this website, your choice will not apply to any other property. Your CCPA opt out right must be exercised on each website of the Walt Disney Family of Companies you access. You or your authorized agent can change your opt out selection anytime by clicking the Do Not Sell My Personal Information link on this site.  Note, third parties may engage in their own sales as defined by the CCPA and you must exercise your CCPA opt out right with each such company separately using this <a href="https://www.iabprivacy.com/optout.html" target="_blank" class="link">link</a>. <br><br>If you choose to opt out of sale of your personal information, you may continue to see advertising, such as ads by us or our partners that are tailored to you and your interests, including, for example, ads that do not involve the sale of personal information or ads based on personal information that was sold before you opted out.  You or your authorized agent may also have other choices and tools that allow you to control certain data collection activities.  To learn more, visit <a href="https://privacy.thewaltdisneycompany.com/en/dnsmi/" target="_blank" class="Do" not="" sell="" my="" personal="" information="" rights="">Do Not Sell My Personal Information Rights</a>.</p></div><!-- Groups sections starts --><!-- Group section ends --><!-- Accordion Group section starts --><!-- Accordion Group section ends --></section></div><section id="ot-pc-lst" class="ot-hide ot-hosts-ui ot-pc-scrollbar ot-enbl-chr"><div id="ot-pc-hdr"><div id="ot-lst-title"><button class="ot-link-btn back-btn-handler" aria-label="Back"><svg id="ot-back-arw" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" x="0px" y="0px" viewBox="0 0 444.531 444.531" xml:space="preserve"><title>Back Button</title><g><path fill="#656565" d="M213.13,222.409L351.88,83.653c7.05-7.043,10.567-15.657,10.567-25.841c0-10.183-3.518-18.793-10.567-25.835
